GT Equivalence Verification (CRK6)

GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_m*sin(sqrt(A))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.4466*A*exp(-0.08660*t) + 0.9910*sin(sqrt(A))`

The GT has two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A*exp(-0.08660*t)` — a product of A and a decaying exponential in t
2. A term proportional to `sin(sqrt(A))` — a sine of square root of A (no t dependence)

Key observations:
- The GT contains `sin(sqrt(A))`, which is a very specific nonlinear function of A
- The GT contains `A*exp(c*t)`, which couples A and t multiplicatively
- No candidate can match unless it can produce both `sin(sqrt(A))` and `A*exp(c*t)` as basis functions

Let me scan through all candidates systematically:

**Candidates with `A*exp(c*t)` term:** 5, 15, 16, 17, 19, 24, 27, 29, 34, 40, 42, 47, 48, 50 (and some others with similar structures)

**Candidates with `sin(sqrt(A))` or equivalent:** None of the candidates explicitly have `sin(sqrt(A))`. Let me check if any candidate can produce this through constant choices.

The function `sin(sqrt(A))` cannot be represented by:
- Polynomials in A (A, A², etc.)
- Rational functions of A (A/(A+c), etc.)
- `exp(c*A)` terms
- `log(A)` terms
- `A^c` power terms (these are monotonic for fixed c)
- `sin(c*log(A*c + 1))` — this is `sin(log(...))`, not `sin(sqrt(...))`
- `Max(0, A)^c/(c + Max(0,A)^c)` — sigmoid-like, not sinusoidal
- `Abs(A)^c` terms

Let me check specific candidates more carefully:

**Candidate 35:** `A²*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)`
This has `sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1))`. For this to equal `sin(sqrt(A))`, we'd need `c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7 = sqrt(A)` for all A, which is impossible since `log` and `sqrt` are linearly independent functions.

Also, the t-dependence is `exp(c3*t)` without A coupling, but GT needs `A*exp(c*t)`.

**Candidate 45:** `A²*c0 + c1*t^c2 + c3 + c4*log(A^c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + 1)`
This has `log(...)` not `sin(sqrt(...))`.

**Candidate 43:** `A^c0*c1 + A^c2*c3 + c4*t/(c5+t²) + c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*t+c9))`
No `sin(sqrt(A))` and no `A*exp(t)` coupling.

After careful analysis, **none** of the candidates contain `sin(sqrt(A))` as a basis function, and this function cannot be algebraically constructed from any combination of the basis functions present in any candidate (polynomials, rationals, exponentials, logarithms, power functions of A). The function `sin(sqrt(A))` is linearly independent from all these.

Therefore, no candidate can match the GT.
